  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }

      AppleID.auth.init({

<span id="freeTextContainer8674780420506648785">The breathtaking action and whirlwind adventure build to a climax in this thrilling conclusion to the “remarkably unpredictable” (BCCB) Sky Fall trilogy from the bestselling author of the Keeper of the Lost Cities series.<br/><br/>Vane Weston is ready for battle. Against Raiden’s army. Against the slowly corrupting Gale Force. Even against his own peaceful nature as a Westerly. He’l</span>
  <span id="freeText8674780420506648785" style="display:none">The breathtaking action and whirlwind adventure build to a climax in this thrilling conclusion to the “remarkably unpredictable” (BCCB) Sky Fall trilogy from the bestselling author of the Keeper of the Lost Cities series.<br /><br />Vane Weston is ready for battle. Against Raiden’s army. Against the slowly corrupting Gale Force. Even against his own peaceful nature as a Westerly. He’ll do whatever it takes, including storming Raiden’s icy fortress with the three people he trusts the least. Anything to bring Audra home safely.<br /><br />But Audra won’t wait for someone to rescue her. She has Gus—the guardian she was captured with. And she has a strange “guide” left behind by the one prisoner who managed to escape Raiden. The wind is also rising to her side, rallying against their common enemy. When the forces align, Audra makes her play—but Raiden is ready.<br /><br />Freedom has never held such an impossible price, and both groups know the sacrifices will be great. But Vane and Audra started this fight together. They’ll end it the same way.</span>

<div id="review_2056429876" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2056429876" />
    <a title="✨    jamieson   ✨" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7706640-jamieson"><img alt="✨    jamieson   ✨" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1499961431p2/7706640.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2056429876?book_show_action=true">Jul 13, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="✨    jamieson   ✨" class="user" itemprop="url" name="✨    jamieson   ✨" href="/user/show/7706640-jamieson">✨    jamieson   ✨</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7706640-jamieson?shelf=2017-reads">2017-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7706640-jamieson?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7706640-jamieson?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7706640-jamieson?shelf=series">series</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2056429876" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8795482004027892294"><b>YOU KNOW</b> that really annoying thing when you know something is a bad idea but your brain is still like <i>dooooo it</i>. Yeah thats me about reading this book <br/><br/><blockquote>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1500042435i/23293290.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</blockquote><br/>(this art is by <a href='walkingnorth.tumblr.com' rel='nofollow noopener'>walkingnorth</a> on tumblr!)<br/><br/><br/><br/><b>
  <u>ANYWAY</u>
</b> me and this series have a pretty rocky relationship. The characters annoyed me so much in book 1, but I stayed in it for the plot. In book 2 the characters got better but the plot fell off. And book 3 ..... everything just burned. <br/><br/><b>I wanted to read this series</b> because it's basically Avatar: Th</span>
  <span id="freeText8795482004027892294" style="display:none"><b>YOU KNOW</b> that really annoying thing when you know something is a bad idea but your brain is still like <i>dooooo it</i>. Yeah thats me about reading this book <br><br><blockquote>
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1500042435i/23293290.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</blockquote><br>(this art is by <a href="walkingnorth.tumblr.com" rel="nofollow noopener">walkingnorth</a> on tumblr!)<br><br><br><br><b>
  <u>ANYWAY</u>
</b> me and this series have a pretty rocky relationship. The characters annoyed me so much in book 1, but I stayed in it for the plot. In book 2 the characters got better but the plot fell off. And book 3 ..... everything just burned. <br><br><b>I wanted to read this series</b> because it's basically Avatar: The Last Airbender plot wise. It's about windwalkers or sylphs, a race of people who have the power to control the wind. There is four different wind groups - the Northerlies, Southerlies, Westerlies and Easterlies ... each controls a different type of wind but live side by side in harmony. AND THEN EVERYTHING CHANGED WHEN RAIDEN ATTACKED. The main character, Vane, is the last Westerly, and he needs to go up against Raiden to save the windwalkers from total destruction. <br><br>So YEAH I was in it for the Avatar plot, and I kinda had hopes for this book because I enjoyed book 2 a bit, <u>but I literally skim read this book from page 200 I was so bored</u><br><br><b>
  <u>WHY I COULDN'T GET INTO THIS </u>
</b><br><br>• <b>Characters.</b> I <i>really</i> didn't like the main character Vane. I found him whiny and annoying for most of it, and his constant inner monologue was <i>really cringeworthy</i> more often then not. He was overly sexual toward the girls in the series and I just found him uncomfortable. I did like that he was an unusual male MC in that he wasn't the gung-ho no feelings fighter manly man type, but I still found him annoying. <br><br>Audra I liked more, and I thought after book 2 she'd have more good character development - but everything just crashed and burned. I genuinely don't think she was in any different place by the end of book 3 then she was in book 1. <br><br>I DID like the side characters, Arella, Aston, Solana, Os and Gus were interesting and they should have been the main characters. <br><br>• <b>SLUT SHAMING. </b> throughout this series, girls who wear short clothes are lusted after because they're "exposing themselves" and are also called skimpy, slutty or skanky. One girl has the power to absorb wind - so the more skin open to the air the better her power. Despite this she's constantly called skanky and skimpy and that annoyed me SO MUCH. It was just unnecessary shaming. I also hated the implication girls who dressed less modest were less honest, more likely to cheat and more likely to "steal yo man", basically. Also, the girls hated on the other girls because of their dress and urghghkd WHY<br><br>• <b>
  <u>PLOT</u>
</b> In this book I found the plot super lacking. For 200 pages literally <i>nothing happens</i> and the end scene wasn't even exciting. I just found it so boring and unsatisfying. The final showdown with the big bad was SO SHORT and it wasn't even dramatic even though he's supposed to be the biggest bad in all the land. <br><br>• <u>
  <b>THE ROMANCE</b>
</u> it was just unconvincing, to me personally. And I found the angst elements of it annoying, there was SO MUCH unnecessary teenage angst I just didn't care about. <br><br>•<u>
  <b>LITERALLY ZERO DIVERSITY</b>
</u><br><br><b>
  <u>MY ONE POSITIVE</u>
</b> I liked the ending. I liked that my favourite character and who I was rooting for got what she deserved. I was pretty satisfied with the conclusion to be honest. <br><br><i>
  <blockquote>"DID YOU SERIOUSLY JUST MISS?" Vane asks.<br>"I TOLD YOU TO GET DOWN!" Aston shouts. "YOU'RE LUCKY I DIDN'T HIT YOUR GIANT SQUARE HEAD!"<br>"I have a square head?" Vane asks.</blockquote>
</i><br><br>Overall this is actually a 1.5 star. Really wouldn't recommend this series to .... anyone really. BUT I have heard good things about Shannon Messenger's other series so she's not cancelled yet, I might check out one of her other series. This one just wasn't for me <u>AT ALL</u><br><br>But I am glad I've finished it at least because yaaaay one more series I can mark as completed.</span>
  <a data-text-id="8795482004027892294" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1299902052" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1299902052" />
    <a title="Anna" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/15725893-anna"><img alt="Anna" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1562029499p2/15725893.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1299902052?book_show_action=true">Jun 05, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Anna" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Anna" href="/user/show/15725893-anna">Anna</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9781481446563" href="/book/show/27221516-let-the-wind-rise">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1299902052" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12532171792197301208"><blockquote>
  <i>"DID YOU SERIOUSLY JUST MISS?" Vane asks.<br/>"I TOLD YOU TO GET DOWN!" Aston shouts. "YOU'RE LUCKY I DIDN'T HIT YOUR GIANT SQUARE HEAD!"<br/>"I have a square head?" Vane asks.</i>
</blockquote><br/>I had to use a quote from probably my favourite character and why not one where you can witness his sass.<br/><br/><b>3 stars for this conclusion so far</b>, because at first I might have rated it even a little lower.<br/><br/>I don't think conclusions help me this year. In other cases it's my too high expectations. In this case, I just felt indifferent t</span>
  <span id="freeText12532171792197301208" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <i>"DID YOU SERIOUSLY JUST MISS?" Vane asks.<br>"I TOLD YOU TO GET DOWN!" Aston shouts. "YOU'RE LUCKY I DIDN'T HIT YOUR GIANT SQUARE HEAD!"<br>"I have a square head?" Vane asks.</i>
</blockquote><br>I had to use a quote from probably my favourite character and why not one where you can witness his sass.<br><br><b>3 stars for this conclusion so far</b>, because at first I might have rated it even a little lower.<br><br>I don't think conclusions help me this year. In other cases it's my too high expectations. In this case, I just felt indifferent to the story...? Maybe?<br><br>The entire book is just two sequences and I was rather bored with the first and the second lost me at some points too.<br>I also didn't care about a few characters and to be specific, it was the females.<br><br>I don't know why but it happened. I didn't care about Solana from the previous book (unecessary drama at points), but Audra lost me as well and I didn't like that. I missed that previous tamed spunk? I felt she was lacking a little in this one? I just didn't feel her.<br><br>And based on my reactions on these two, I became indifferent (not always) on Vane too. And that's even more sad because I like Vane. I like that he isn't the typical macho guy that fears nothing and just masters the techniques 20 pages in, but he is in fact senitive and scared most of the time and pretty sarcastic. And I love his reactions. But he was dragged down by the others. And the romance might have been all over the place.<br><br>On the other hand, though I loved Aston (who I still can't remember in book 2) and Gus. I think that <b>crucial part</b> that stars Gus made me feel something for the first time while reading this book and with Aston I just loved his many shades. And he was probably my favourite character by the end of the book.<br><br>I don't know. I still feel confused about my experience reading this. Perhaps if I read it at another time, I might have enjoyed it more, but right now I feel it was a nice conclusion but nothing that will leave everlasting effects on me.<br><br>And that's a shame because the concept was pretty unique for me, since I hadn't read (and still haven't) a similar book (in terms of windwalkers and such) before.<br>Maybe a re-read in the distant future will be required.<br><br><b>Pre-read:</b><br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[WE HAVE A DESCRIPTION.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/497460.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>_________________________________<br><br>I like the cover as an independent one, because I don't think it matches that much the other two.<br><br>Where is my description, though? <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_1091667077" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1091667077" />
    <a title="Ally" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7206156-ally"><img alt="Ally" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/f_50x66-6a03a5c12233c941481992b82eea8d23.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1091667077?book_show_action=true">Oct 28, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ally" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ally" href="/user/show/7206156-ally">Ally</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Hardcover 9781481446549" href="/book/show/25785671-let-the-wind-rise">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
                  <em>
                    This review has been hidden because it contains spoilers. To view it,
                    <a href="#" onclick="Effect.toggle(&#39;reviewTextContainer1091667077&#39;); return false;">click here.</a>
                  </em>
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1091667077" class="readable"
                    style="display:none"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer383039187909339090">This book is very different from the others. They gripped you and held you at the edge of your seat. I did not feel that with this one.<br/> One major problem I had in this book was the ending. Raiden's defeat was low-key to say the least. Also, Audra had training and sacrificed so much to avenge her father and keep Vane safe. The end goal for her was always to be able to defeat Raiden, she was even willing to sacrifice her own life to defeat him. Then, Messenger decides for her to sit home and wait </span>
  <span id="freeText383039187909339090" style="display:none">This book is very different from the others. They gripped you and held you at the edge of your seat. I did not feel that with this one.<br /> One major problem I had in this book was the ending. Raiden's defeat was low-key to say the least. Also, Audra had training and sacrificed so much to avenge her father and keep Vane safe. The end goal for her was always to be able to defeat Raiden, she was even willing to sacrifice her own life to defeat him. Then, Messenger decides for her to sit home and wait for her man to return from battle. A terrible decision really. She built the trilogy for Vane, Audra, and Solane to defeat him-they all had the most reasons/grief over Raiden's actions and should be the ones to see him dead. All four of the new rulers should have fought him to show unity. Instead, Audra sat and had everyone else fight her for. Which was very disappointing for me and was unrealistic to the story line.<br /> Another thing that bothered me was Messenger's overuse of short paragraphs, all capital words, and italics. I get that short paragraphs and italics are an effective way to showcase a important sentence or way to empathize something to the reader. But when she used those devices three times in two pages it got annoying fast.<br /> Overall, this was not the book I thought it would be.</span>
  <a data-text-id="383039187909339090" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27474332-tanja?shelf=did-not-finish">did-not-finish</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1669120098" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4962563267253109601">09-25-16: page 105, DNF'ed it.<br/><br/>I wasn't too wow-ed by the first two books, but I flew through them which made it easier. This one on the other hand...<br/><br/>Maybe it's because 2016 just hasn't been a very good reading year so far, maybe it's because I decided that life's too short for crappy books, maybe it's because this book simply is really badly written...<br/><br/>I mean, c'mon... the plot's so thin it's almost non-existent. The characters are two-dimensional at best, but mostly they're just shells of gender</span>
  <span id="freeText4962563267253109601" style="display:none">09-25-16: page 105, DNF'ed it.<br /><br />I wasn't too wow-ed by the first two books, but I flew through them which made it easier. This one on the other hand...<br /><br />Maybe it's because 2016 just hasn't been a very good reading year so far, maybe it's because I decided that life's too short for crappy books, maybe it's because this book simply is really badly written...<br /><br />I mean, c'mon... the plot's so thin it's almost non-existent. The characters are two-dimensional at best, but mostly they're just shells of gender-stereotypical, immature seemingly 15 but probably meant to be older. The only one mildly interesting is Arella yet she’s dismissed as an evil, betraying piece of shit who isn’t worth more than a second glance. That’s an interesting perception which could have been a great spin on the “plot”, but it’s just left at snappy comments and “winds being thrown at her.” I’m so tired of winds being thrown around, it’s literally all that happens in this book. That and Vane being a 10-year old with the vocabulary of a 7-year old. <br />I find it hard to even have opinions about this book, that’s how little it excites and interests me. I hate to see a trilogy end like this, even if it wasn’t a very strong one to begin with. <br /></span>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2438316152" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2438316152" />
    <a title="Valery" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/35798331-valery"><img alt="Valery" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1477279647p2/35798331.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2438316152?book_show_action=true">Jul 05, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Valery" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Valery" href="/user/show/35798331-valery">Valery</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2438316152" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2439081818736524031">3.5 stars. It was a good read. Good, not great. I would still recommend it when one is looking for a time killer.<br/><br/>The good:<br/>Vane grew up a lot in this book. He isn't as whiney and he definitely learned to take charge. The climax was as expected. There weren't any weird twists that made you leap out of your seat with manic frustration, nor was there anything that broke the author/reader contract. I actually liked the turn of events with Arella too.<br/><br/>Now for the gripes:<br/>Am I the only one who feels as i</span>
  <span id="freeText2439081818736524031" style="display:none">3.5 stars. It was a good read. Good, not great. I would still recommend it when one is looking for a time killer.<br /><br />The good:<br />Vane grew up a lot in this book. He isn't as whiney and he definitely learned to take charge. The climax was as expected. There weren't any weird twists that made you leap out of your seat with manic frustration, nor was there anything that broke the author/reader contract. I actually liked the turn of events with Arella too.<br /><br />Now for the gripes:<br />Am I the only one who feels as if Audra turned from tough guardian to wimpy damsel in distress? I understand that torture changes you, but it felt as if she became a completely different person, as if she and Solana changed places in some sort of weird brain swap. I don't know, it just felt strange to me.<br /><br />I also found a couple more grammar mistakes than the last one. Missing words, lost punctuation...man, I feel like I should be on a grammar treasure hunt when I read such things. Oh where, oh where did your quotation marks go? Did they magically disappear in the conversion process to ebook? Or did it get lost in editing?<br /><br />Anyway, it was still a decent read.<br /><br />For my clean readers:<br />Mild language, violence, torture in both physical and mental forms, sexual nuances but no follow through or descriptions, insinuation of possible rape, and murder.</span>
  <a data-text-id="2439081818736524031" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1603839788" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1603839788" />
    <a title="Jessica (Books: A true story)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1113710-jessica-books-a-true-story"><img alt="Jessica (Books: A true story)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1498713175p2/1113710.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1603839788?book_show_action=true">Apr 07, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jessica (Books: A true story)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jessica (Books: A true story)" href="/user/show/1113710-jessica-books-a-true-story">Jessica (Books: A true story)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Hardcover 9781481446549" href="/book/show/25785671-let-the-wind-rise">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113710-jessica-books-a-true-story?shelf=own">own</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113710-jessica-books-a-true-story?shelf=instagram-review">instagram-review</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113710-jessica-books-a-true-story?shelf=amazon">amazon</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113710-jessica-books-a-true-story?shelf=blog">blog</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113710-jessica-books-a-true-story?shelf=hardcover">hardcover</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113710-jessica-books-a-true-story?shelf=3-stars">3-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113710-jessica-books-a-true-story?shelf=gift">gift</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1603839788" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16489319929657054861">The characters are my favorite thing about this series. The plot was a little lacking in this third book. No twists. No turns. No surprises. It was a good plot it just didn't have that wow factor. The first book was the best, but you'll want to know what happens to these characters despite the plot getting lamer as it goes.<br/><br/> Vane still has a great, sarcastic voice with some self-deprecating humor. The romance didn't have the spark that I remember them having in the other books but I still really </span>
  <span id="freeText16489319929657054861" style="display:none">The characters are my favorite thing about this series. The plot was a little lacking in this third book. No twists. No turns. No surprises. It was a good plot it just didn't have that wow factor. The first book was the best, but you'll want to know what happens to these characters despite the plot getting lamer as it goes.<br /><br /> Vane still has a great, sarcastic voice with some self-deprecating humor. The romance didn't have the spark that I remember them having in the other books but I still really like their relationship. She helps him be brave and he helps her think about what she really wants instead of just following the rules all the time. I like that Vane is not a stereotypical brooding romantic interest. He's actually sweet, obeys his parents, tries not to swear, doesn't like violence, but still acts like a confident and hormonal teenager. Here's some of Vane's self-deprecating humor:<br /><br />"Actually, 'uncomfortable' isn't a strong enough word. This is like if awkward and uncomfortable hooked up and had an ugly, miserable baby that won't stop screaming and pooping all over everything." -pg 158. I'm telling you that happened to me yesterday.<br /><br />Learning about the villain's background was cool but it didn't really go anywhere either. At the end, the background they learned played zero role in their plan to defeat him. So I'm not sure what the point of that was.<br /><br />The theme in this book was faith and trust vs. pain and which was more powerful. It was an interesting concept. After finishing the book, I would say that pain has an immediate and strong power but it just doesn't last long. Faith and trust are more enduring and therefore more powerful. <br /><br />I like the magic system. Winds that can sing real words to those that can understand them and those words have magical powers is so beautiful. I also liked how Shannon used real wind storm names in her book. Did you know that simoons and haboobs are real storms? Me neither. And Vane is immature enough to laugh at the word "haboob" and that's why I love him.</span>
  <a data-text-id="16489319929657054861" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

I'm so happy this mess is over.<br/><br/>It really makes me sad how much I disliked this series. I love Keepers to death and was expecting a grand YA adventure in this series.<br/><br/>Instead I got the usual YA tropes...<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1389385904ra/8026998.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>...with a male protag. <br/><br/>Honestly, this book brought nothing new. I love Keepers to death and was expecting a grand YA adventure in this series.<br><br>Instead I got the usual YA tropes...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1389385904ra/8026998.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>...with a male protag. <br><br>Honestly, this book brought nothing new. I was begging, begging for Audra to show off the amazing skills that she apparently had.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1473194023ra/20425101.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Spoiler alert, it doesn't happen. Like...whut.<br><br>Also, like always male gaze is in full effect to the point it doesn't make sense.<br><br>These slyph are used to showing skin. WHY DOES SOLANA AND AUDRA FEEL AWKWARD AROUND VANE STARING AT THEM. He was staring at their legs, ect. Aka, body parts that both should be okay with showing.<br><br>That was downright infuriating for me.<br><br>I can't even really talk about the ending because I was skimming for most of it because I just could not take it anymore. <br><br>So....when is Lodestar coming out?<br><br></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer291482421311139855">If I thought book 2 was disappointing, imagine what Let the Wind Rise is... First of all, what is with the unnecessary cover change? Honestly, Gus was the only good character. <br/><br/>Sorry Shanno</span>
  <span id="freeText291482421311139855" style="display:none">If I thought book 2 was disappointing, imagine what Let the Wind Rise is... First of all, what is with the unnecessary cover change? The original covers were okay, but this looks like a Percy Jackson cover. Vane is <i>not</i> Percy Jackson no matter how hard you try, Shannon Messenger. Second of all, Audra is officially no longer interesting. I try not to think about her anymore. Vane tries to be funny but fails and ends up sounding really stupid. Honestly, Gus was the only good character. <br /><br />Sorry Shannon Messenger, you're a good middle-grade writer but you just can't write YA. </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer918474749" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13975967095590942449">This was a nice ending to a series I really enjoyed. As always, I loved Vane's humor and Aston's snark was a nice addition too.<br/><br/>I did have trouble keeping track of Vane and Audra's chapters though. For some reason their narrative voices felt too similar this time.</span>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('mH1Sv7DgG2CQxVZqgtLCa/YFWp0d61iCElhLENHMjOmRfN9TgBFhwRZYisqbmwMf85jz5pQ+BPi71j466Jjngw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('JcDF6/Dn9H4HOg2651Hfi+WyjxEo29OkNMfqi/BG48sswUgHwBaO34Gn0Rr+GB7/4C8maqEOj96dSZ+hyRKIoQ==')})
  }
